texlive-montserrat in Fedora 34

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of texlive-montserrat. You might want go back to the main page of texlive-montserrat.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-03-08 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-38 - update texlive-subfiles and fix dependencies
2021-01-27 Fedora Release Engineering - 9:2020-37 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_34_Mass_Rebuild
2020-12-15 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-36 - restore the ".0" at the end of the arphic version string to fix clean update path
2020-12-07 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-35 - put the /usr/share/fonts/tex-gyre symlink back in
2020-11-23 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-34 - do not make fonts symlink for texlive-merriweather (sorkintype-merriweather-fonts is in Fedora)
2020-11-16 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-33 - texlive-optex moves to texlive-base (where it should have been)
2020-11-10 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-32 - fix platex file ownership
2020-11-02 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-31 - update the following fonts: * algolrevived * almendra * baskervillef * bitter * cabin * cochineal * domitian * erewhon * etbb * fbb * forum * garamond-libre * libertinus * libertinus-fonts * libertinus-otf * libertinus-type1 * libertinust1math * librebaskerville * librecaslon * lobster2 * marcellus * merriweather * newtx * newtxsf * overlock * playfair * quattrocento * scholax * xcharter - add these new fonts: * cmathbb * courierten * ibarra * josefin * notomath * plimsoll * spectral - and update the default font map files to match (texlive-updmap-map)
2020-10-23 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-30 - move all the big Obsoletes over to fedora-obsolete-packages
2020-10-23 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-29 - drop Requires: texlive-obsoletes (so fedora-obsolete-packages can handle it)
